<div id="theReview">
<h2>I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)</h2>
<p class="ratd"> Rated <em>MA</em></p>
<p><em>Review by Margaret Pomeranz</em></p>
<p>One of the highlights of last year's Venice Film Festival for me was Io Sono L'Amore, I AM LOVE, starring TILDA SWINTON as Emma, the Russian-born wife of a Milan industrialist, Tancredi Recchi - PIPPO DELBONO. She lives in a most beautiful house, has two sons and a daughter. Her main tasks seem to be picking up the dry-cleaning and arranging the table at dinner parties. Her son Edo - FLAVIO PARENTI, who co-inherits the family business with his father, introduces her to his friend Antonio - EDOARDO GABBRIELLINI - a young chef with dreams of opening his own restaurant in the countryside......<br/><br/>There is no stopping the affair between Emma and Antonio, even though both know how dangerous it is. Like all lovers, the world is their own when they're together...<br/><br/>This is Italian melodrama at its most exquisite. Writer/Director Luca Guadagnino draws us into this world of luxury, filling in small details of Emma's life so that within the golden cage there is a sense of being trapped, a sense of displacement or misplacement. And when tragedy strikes he shows enormous restraint in its presentation. There are wonderful performances from the entire cast but TILDA SWINTON is really something, she shares so much with an audience by seemingly doing so very little. <br/><br/>There are other stories within the film, the potential sale of the Recchi business is another indication that this world will not last, and Betta, the daughter, beautifully played by ALBA ROHRWACHER, has her own agenda that may not fit in with her father's expectations. This is a beautiful film, moving, stylish with a sensual romance at its heart.</p>
<h2>Further comments</h2>
<p>COMMENTS ARE NOT AVAILABLE AT THE MOMENT.</p>

<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[9]]<br>I'm surprised by the negative comments, I thought this film was fascinating on many levels. The photography was so sensitive I found myself responding emotionally even when just looking at people's backs. I would call this film an artwork. It is visually, intellectually and spiritually moving and like slow food, slow film is so nourishing and so rare in a sea of syrupy American romance and action films.</br></p>

<h3>Leigh :</h3>
<p class="date">13 Nov 2010 9:49:12am</p>
<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[6]]<br>I didn't feel the love for Lo Sono L'Amore! It is an exquisite and stylish film with a very believable performance from Tilda Swinton yet it failed to connect with me on an emotional level. The interior features of this film are extremely minutiae in depiction but the exterior of the film is very tacitly approached, particularly the closing scene's. I therefore found I am Love's music score to be over-dramatised and felt little compassion for most of the characters. I liken this film to last years "The Reader", Good, yes but highly over-rated. 3 stars from me!</br></p>

<h3>Greg :</h3>
<p class="date">14 Aug 2010 11:39:22pm</p>
<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[8]]<br>At first I thought the film to be a little boring but as it developed I became more and more intrigued by the subtlety and contrasts within the film both in the settings and musical score. A film truly in the modern Italian genre. Like 'Stealing Beauty' the film used settings, sounds and food to paint an truly thoughtful and highly intelligent film of modern Italy. It was a film of such strange contradictions it took great skill to weave this tapestry of history, love, grief and family. <br>Let yourself languish in this exquisite piece of Italian Cinema.</br></br></p>
<p class="links">
<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141229131517/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/AlertModerator.aspx?b=117&amp;m=2681&amp;tpa=&amp;r=%2ftmb%2fView%2fMessage.aspx%3fb%3d117%26t%3d90%26a%3d0%26ps%3d50%26tpa%3d%26uto%3d1%26dm%3d4%26ci%3d0%26pd%3d1%26so%3dDateTime%26soa%3dFalse%26p%3d1%26p2%3d0" onclick="return popup(this.href);">Alert moderator</a>

<a id="m_ucMessageDisplay2614_m_anchMessageAnchor" name="m2614"></a>
<h3>Haden Young :</h3>
<p class="date">11 Aug 2010 12:32:16am</p>
<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[6]]<br>I had a feeling the title wasn't the literal translation and I just put it through the AltaVista Babelfish translator and sure enough, Il Sono L'amore translates to "They Are Love". Nice title, and sure enough, completely changes the connotation and meaning. I find the interpretations or modifications given to us by translators a little patronising, as I find sometimes when watching French films,a language I speak. To those who thought the title was pretentious, well there you go,it wasn't. "They Are Love" is much softer, rolls of the tongue much better and makes more sense.</br></p>
<p class="links">
<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141229131517/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/AlertModerator.aspx?b=117&amp;m=2614&amp;tpa=&amp;r=%2ftmb%2fView%2fMessage.aspx%3fb%3d117%26t%3d90%26a%3d0%26ps%3d50%26tpa%3d%26uto%3d1%26dm%3d4%26ci%3d0%26pd%3d1%26so%3dDateTime%26soa%3dFalse%26p%3d1%26p2%3d0" onclick="return popup(this.href);">Alert moderator</a>

<h3>Haden Young :</h3>
<p class="date">29 Jul 2010 5:36:58pm</p>
<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[6]]<br>This film looked very pretty and was finely acted and on the whole well-directed. Directorial style was a little stodgy and rigid to my tastes though, so that the film barely touched me emotionally mostly. I felt like I was looking at a very pretty piece of cardboard. Its insights into the latent lethality of bitchy, cattily competitive upper  upper-middle class life was masterfully assured though, but still, it failed to be emotionally convincing to me. I'm surprised David &amp; Margaret'd buy into this kind of somewhat shallow bourgeois entertainment, but then maybe that stands to reason...</br></p>

<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[9]]<br/>It feels like opera. It looks like Dynasty. It is about splendour, soup and sex and it is fantastic. I loved the sex scene with the bugs and the heat, raw and tremendously passionate. I enjoyed that nothing is spelled out, yet so clear to those who  understand. <a id="m_ucMessageDisplay2057_m_anchMessageAnchor" name="m2057"></a>
<h3>Jude :</h3>
<p class="date">18 Jul 2010 1:14:11am</p>
<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[9]]<br/>It's been fascinating reading these polarised reviews! And so bizarre to read that audiences laughed at the end. I loved the bold cinematic gestures of this film.  The stylised elements contrasted beautifully with the subtleties of the film. The power of this film comes from what is suggested. There are reactions we aren't shown. There is much unsaid and many narrative ambiguities but this is what creates an intensity that is so delicious. This is a very intelligent and thought-provoking film indeed. The sort of film I could happily see again.</p>
<p class="links">
<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141229131517/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/AlertModerator.aspx?b=117&amp;m=2057&amp;tpa=&amp;r=%2ftmb%2fView%2fMessage.aspx%3fb%3d117%26t%3d90%26a%3d0%26ps%3d50%26tpa%3d%26uto%3d1%26dm%3d4%26ci%3d0%26pd%3d1%26so%3dDateTime%26soa%3dFalse%26p%3d1%26p2%3d0" onclick="return popup(this.href);">Alert moderator</a>

<h3>Anthony Abrahams :</h3>
<p class="date">11 Jul 2010 12:12:52am</p>
<p class="comment">((I Am Love (Io Sono L'amore)))[[4]]<br/>The film walks a fine line between the operatic and the false. Years ago, during my 24 years of life in France I felt  on visits home, that David saw Europe through slightly parochial glasses and was too tolerant of some very self conscious or pretentious films from France. A week or two each May on La Croisette is no way to gain a healthy understanding of the deeper side of France or of its less worthy efforts in the cinema.  Here we have an Italian version of the same shortcoming.. In the balance this film will not endure..</p>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">


var newtopicKey;

$(document).ready(function(){

audShow();
changeAction();
formatComments();

// end ready
});	

function audShow() {
	// display word count only if js enabled
	document.getElementById("wordCount").style.display='inline';
	document.getElementById("audiencecomment").style.display='block';
	if (document.getElementById("allnewComments")) {
		document.getElementById("allnewComments").innerHTML = document.getElementById("loadComments").innerHTML;
	}
}


function changeAction() {
	// avoids non-js form submission 
	var tmpStoryid = "??StoryID??";
	if (document.m_frmMainForm) {
		document.m_frmMainForm.action = 'https://web.archive.org/web/20141229131517/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/NewMessage.aspx?b=117&amp;tn='+tmpStoryid+'&amp;dm=1&amp;tpa=&amp;r=&amp;layout=popup';
		}
}



function formatComments() {
	// replace H3 tag with 'Name:' + name
	var arrayH3 = document.getElementById("comments").getElementsByTagName("h3");
	for (var i = 0; i < arrayH3.length; i++) {
		var theString = arrayH3[i].innerHTML;
		theString = theString.replace(":", "");
		theString = "Name: "+theString;
		arrayH3[i].innerHTML = 	theString;
	}
	// add rating value to each comment
	var arrayComment = getElementsByClassName( 'comment', 'p' );	
	for (var c = 0; c < arrayComment.length; c++) {
		var theComment = arrayComment[c].innerHTML;
		theComment = theComment.replace("[[", "<span class='userRating'>Rating: <img src='https://web.archive.org/web/20141229131517/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/audience/stars").replace("]]",".png' alt='rating'></span>").replace("((", "<!-- ").replace(")))", "))").replace("))", "-->");
		arrayComment[c].innerHTML = theComment;
	}

	
}


function formCheck(zeForm) {
	// pass key to form
	document.getElementById("keyField").value = newtopicKey;
	// basic validation
	if (document.getElementById("yname").value.length < 1) {
		alert("Please enter your name or nickname.");
		document.getElementById("yname").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;
	}
	if (document.getElementById("yemail").value.length < 6) {
		alert("Please enter a valid email address.");
		document.getElementById("yemail").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;
	}
	if (zeForm.score.options[0].selected && zeForm.score.options[0].value=="na") {
		alert("You forgot to rate the movie!");
		document.getElementById("score").style.background='#FFFDC8';	
		return false;
	}	
	// check for http
	spamcheck=zeForm.m_tbxText.value;
	if (spamcheck.indexOf("http")!=-1) {
		document.m_frmMainForm.action = 'https://web.archive.org/web/20141229131517/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/audience/blank.htm';
	}
	// check word count
	wct = cnt(zeForm.m_tbxText.value);
	if (wct > 100) {
		alert("Comments are limited to 100 words. You've written "+wct+" words!");
		document.getElementById("remark").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;	
	}
	
	// replace usual suspect bad characters 
	badChars = Array  ('', '', '', '', '', 'ö', 'é', 'è', 'ñ', 'â', ' ', '','','´');
	goodChars = Array ('...', '-', '-', '"', '"', 'o', 'e', 'e', 'n', 'a', ' ', '\'','\'','\'');
	fld = document.getElementById("remark");
	for(i=0;i<badChars.length;i++){
		restring = new RegExp( badChars[i] , 'g');
		fld.value = fld.value.replace(restring,goodChars[i]);
	}
	fldn = document.getElementById("yname");
	for(j=0;j<badChars.length;j++){
		restringj = new RegExp( badChars[j] , 'g');
		fldn.value = fldn.value.replace(restringj,goodChars[j]);
	}	
	
	// add rating to comment field in [[ ]] tags 
	var theSel = zeForm.score.selectedIndex;
	var theRating = zeForm.score[theSel].value; 
	zeForm.m_tbxText.value = "[["+theRating+"]]\n" + zeForm.m_tbxText.value;
	
	// add movie title to comment field in (( )) tags 
	zeForm.m_tbxText.value = "(("+theMovie+"))" + zeForm.m_tbxText.value;	
	
	// display thankyou div layer and hide form. 
	document.getElementById("favFormThx").style.display='block';
	document.getElementById("favForm").style.display='none';
	document.getElementById("wordCount").style.display='none';	
	
	// all clear, submit the form
	return true;
}

// word count function
function cnt(theform){
	var y=theform;
	var r = 0;
	a=y.replace('\n',' ');
	a=a.split(' ');
	for (z=0; z<a.length; z++) {if (a[z].length > 0) r++;}
	return r;
}

function remainingWords(textAreaContent,textAreaContentValue, maxWords) 
{
	// Determine the number of words we have left
	var numberofwords = cnt(textAreaContentValue);
	wordsLeft = maxWords - numberofwords;
	if (wordsLeft < 1)
	{	// if 100 change color to red
		document.getElementById("wcNum").style.color='red'; 
	} else {
		document.getElementById("wcNum").style.color='#ffffff'; 
	}
	// update word count number
	document.getElementById("wcNum").innerHTML=(0+numberofwords);
}

// windows media alt box
function showWindows() {
	document.getElementById("windowsMed").style.display='block';
}


// generic get by class name
function getElementsByClassName(strClass, strTag, objContElm) {
  strTag = strTag || "*";
  objContElm = objContElm || document;    
  var objColl = objContElm.getElementsByTagName(strTag);
  if (!objColl.length &&  strTag == "*" &&  objContElm.all) objColl = objContElm.all;
  var arr = new Array();                              
  var delim = strClass.indexOf('|') != -1  ? '|' : ' ';   
  var arrClass = strClass.split(delim);    
  for (var i = 0, j = objColl.length; i < j; i++) {                         
    var arrObjClass = objColl[i].className.split(' ');   
    if (delim == ' ' && arrClass.length > arrObjClass.length) continue;
    var c = 0;
    comparisonLoop:
    for (var k = 0, l = arrObjClass.length; k < l; k++) {
      for (var m = 0, n = arrClass.length; m < n; m++) {
        if (arrClass[m] == arrObjClass[k]) c++;
        if ((delim == '|' && c == 1) || (delim == ' ' && c == arrClass.length)) {
          arr.push(objColl[i]); 
          break comparisonLoop;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return arr; 
}

// called from 'new discussion' page in iframe
function sayHello(theKey) {
	newtopicKey = theKey;
}

// talk to www2b iframe
document.domain = "abc.net.au";

		//mobile device supports m3u8 html5 HLS video
